< Text>
Great hike with a beautiful view. If you plan to hike this trail, please wear proper hiking shoes  to avoid injuries. Also, I know everyone loves thier pets, but these trails are not for pets and offer little to no shade. Therefore, please leave your pets at home, where they can be comfortable and safe. In addition, take your trash out with you. A few people are leaving water bottles and mask on the trails (No Bueno). Furthermore, if you are hiking to the swim cave, please be extremely safe and come prepared with plenty of water and proper hiking attire.
I do not recommend this hike for anyone with existing injuries, pets or children.
Enjoy nature and remain safe.

See you on the trails.</Text>

This place is the home of the hidden swing. In order to get to the hidden swing take a left off the main trail and follow the mountain bike trail all the way. You will see a white rabbit spray painted. Follow the white rabbit until you get to apes spray painted purple. Take a right and go up the trail until you get to Gatsby spray painted. Gatsby will lead you down to the hidden swing. Please pick up your trash and leave the area better than you found it.

Some good SoCal day hiking... Trail is a loop.

If you're trying to get to the cave/swing, take the right side for a more gradual incline (but long route) or the left foot a way shorter, steeper route.

And please, please  keep to the social distancing and no littering rules. This has only gotten super popular during the pandemic and there's a real fear of it being eventually shut down if people aren't careful about this. üò∞ (And it's such an awesome spot! Would be a shame)< /Text>

<userid>116405199766847805352< /userid>< username>
Hollie O'Brien<//username>
< date>
1598718491139<//date>
<Rating>3</Rating>< Text>
It's a little sketchy trying to find parking. Go to the end of the road between where it says begin and end "no parking" and you can park on the side of the road. A lot of things I read online beforehand said you could park in the dirt road that's right off the 118 exit but I don't recommend going off-roading there mostly because when people pave the road they left the curb that you'll have to drive over. It is a very steep and bike heavy trail. It's beautiful the earlier you go but be warned almost got ran off the trail multiple times by bikes without bells. There is a swing that is overly popular with the Instagram models. Don't go up the hummingbird trail but go left when you hit the first split. and then follow the graffiti all the way up to the overrated swing. Overall a little sketchy and steep but a nice morning walk. I'm not sure if I would come here again. It was worth a try and I would give it five stars based on the views alone. I wish people would pick up their trash and not graffiti the rocks everywhere.< /Text>

<review>This hike can be pretty steep, and past the 1 mile mark there are many different trails that for the most part, end up meeting. If you plan on finishing the trail, it is easy to pass the last part of the trail leading up. There are trail marks on the floor to help guide you,  so be mindful of your surroundings.

This is a trail used by mountain bikers and hikers and runners, so be mindful of each other. PLEASE BRING A TRASH BAG FOR YOUR TRASH, and try to bring back one piece of trash that isn't yours. It's greatly appreciated.

From your friendly Adventure 16 member,
Joe Flores

They offer a genetic test that shows which medications will work best for each individual and which medications to stay away from. This takes the guess work out of the equation which means no more "start on these and we will see how they work for you, if they don't work we will randomly try a different medication". That process can take months to years before finding "what works". Instead they just sent the matter to collections with no follow up with me and when the bill collector contacted me, they made me do the legwork to prove I had paid the bill. Once I provided the paperwork, they were unapologetic and made excuses for their utter lack or professionalism. DON'T WASTE YOUR TIME WITH THIS FACILITY! Between the awful therapist and the horrible billing and admin staff, everything about this place made for a horrible experience and a complete waste of time.</review>
